# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 23:13:17.680877

### Base Program

```py
def find_pivot(n: int) -> int:
    total = n * (n + 1) // 2
    left_sum = 0
    for x in range(1, n + 1):
        left_sum += x
        if 2 * left_sum == total:
            return x
    return -1
```

### Input

```json
[28]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def find_pivot(n: int) -> int:
    total = n * (n + 1) // 2
    left_sum = 0
    for x in range(1, n + 1):
        left_sum += x
        if 2 * left_sum == total:
            return x
    return -1
```

<details>

Success

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def find_pivot(var_0: int) -> int:
    total = var_0 * (var_0 + 1) // 2
    left_sum = 0
    for x in range(1, var_0 + 1):
        left_sum += x
        if 2 * left_sum == total:
            return x
    return -1
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def find_pivot(n: int) -> int:
    total = (1 + n) * n // 2
    left_sum = 0
    for x in range(1, 1 + n):
        left_sum += x
        if left_sum * 2 == total:
            return x
    return -1
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def find_pivot(var_1: int) -> int:
    total = (1 + var_1) * var_1 // 2
    left_sum = 0
    for x in range(1, 1 + var_1):
        left_sum += x
        if left_sum * 2 == total:
            return x
    return -1
```
